about_this_resource_text: <h2 class="subhead">Description</h2> <p>This lecture introduced
  the fundamental knowledge and basic principles of airplane aerodynamics.</p> <p><strong>Instructor:&nbsp;</strong>Philip
  Greenspun, Tina Srisvastava</p>

  <span m="1729100">the</span> <span m="1729250">air</span> <span m="1729490">is</span>
  <span m="1729640">moving</span> <span m="1730510">very</span> <span m="1730840">smoothly</span>
  <span m="1731890">past</span> <span m="1732970">the</span> <span m="1733240">airfoil,</span>
  <span m="1734230">then</span> <span m="1734470">it's</span> <span m="1734620">very</span>
  <span m="1734920">easy</span> <span m="1735400">to</span> <span m="1735520">come</span>
  <span m="1735820">up--</span> <span m="1736240">not</span> <span m="1736450">easy,</span>
  <span m="1736870">but</span> <span m="1737050">it's</span> <span m="1737290">easier</span>

  <span m="1741280">molecule</span> <span m="1741940">is</span> <span m="1742090">going</span>
  <span m="1742360">to</span> <span m="1742510">do.</span></p><p><span m="1743260">But</span>

  <span m="2697140">so</span> <span m="2697290">your</span> <span m="2697470">induced</span>
  <span m="2697950">drag</span> <span m="2698910">decreases.</span></p><p><span m="2700580">Now,</span>
  <span m="2700680">with</span> <span m="2700800">the</span> <span m="2700920">induced</span>
  <span m="2701280">drag</span> <span m="2701580">decreases,</span> <span m="2702210">it's</span>
  <span m="2702390">actually</span> <span m="2702750">the</span> <span m="2702870">case</span>
  <span m="2703410">that</span> <span m="2703620">your</span> <span m="2703830">airplane</span>
  <span m="2704700">can</span> <span m="2704880">become</span> <span m="2705390">airborne</span>
  <span m="2706710">at</span> <span m="2706860">a</span> <span m="2706920">lower</span>
  <span m="2708210">speed</span> <span m="2708690">than</span> <span m="2708900">it's</span>
  <span m="2708990">supposed</span> <span m="2709470">to.</span> <span m="2710010">So</span>
  <span m="2710190">what</span> <span m="2710430">you</span> <span m="2710550">might</span>
  <span m="2710760">notice</span> <span m="2711210">is</span> <span m="2711390">that</span>

  <span m="2713160">the</span> <span m="2713250">runway</span> <span m="2714090">taking</span>
  <span m="2714540">off--</span> <span m="2714780">this is</span> <span m="2714900">probably</span>

  <span m="2918140">you're</span> <span m="2919070">not</span> <span m="2919430">turning</span>
  <span m="2920210">the</span> <span m="2920360">rudder</span> <span m="2920720">in</span>
  <span m="2920810">the</span> <span m="2920900">same</span> <span m="2921230">direction</span>

  <span m="2924800">so</span> <span m="2925010">this</span> <span m="2925280">is</span>
  <span m="2925490">where</span> <span m="2926000">you</span> <span m="2926150">talk</span>

  <span m="2929210">When</span> <span m="2929360">you're</span> <span m="2929480">actually</span>
  <span m="2929870">in</span> <span m="2930080">an</span> <span m="2930230">airplane,</span>
  <span m="2931250">the</span> <span m="2931490">rudder</span> <span m="2932420">or</span>
  <span m="2932540">the</span> <span m="2932690">yaw</span> <span m="2933530">is</span>
  <span m="2933740">controlled</span> <span m="2934130">by</span> <span m="2934250">your</span>
  <span m="2934400">feet.</span> <span m="2934800">So</span> <span m="2934970">you</span>
  <span m="2935060">have</span> <span m="2935180">feet</span> <span m="2935480">pedals</span>
  <span m="2936980">that</span> <span m="2937130">control</span> <span m="2937810">the</span>
  <span m="2938180">rudder.</span> <span m="2938930">And</span> <span m="2939590">the</span>
  <span m="2939920">yoke</span> <span m="2940700">that</span> <span m="2940910">you're</span>
  <span m="2941000">holding</span> <span m="2941360">onto</span> <span m="2941810">or</span>
  <span m="2941930">a</span> <span m="2941990">joystick</span> <span m="2942560">that</span>
  <span m="2942740">you're</span> <span m="2942830">holding</span> <span m="2943160">onto</span>
  <span m="2943940">front</span> <span m="2944300">and</span> <span m="2944420">back</span>
  <span m="2944690">controls</span> <span m="2945620">the</span> <span m="2945740">pitch.</span>
  <span m="2947210">And</span> <span m="2947360">then</span> <span m="2947810">turning</span>
  <span m="2948260">it</span> <span m="2948780">like</span> <span m="2949080">in</span>
  <span m="2949240">the</span> <span m="2949310">steering</span> <span m="2949760">wheel</span>

  <span m="2950540">is</span> <span m="2950780">only</span> <span m="2951050">controlling</span>
  <span m="2951950">the</span> <span m="2952100">roll.</span> <span m="2952700">So</span>

  <span m="3376090">you're</span> <span m="3376210">also</span> <span m="3376570">not</span>
  <span m="3377170">accelerating.</span></p><p><span m="3381500">Now,</span> <span
  m="3381910">this</span> <span m="3382270">is</span> <span m="3382420">a</span> <span
  m="3382480">little</span> <span m="3382720">bit</span> <span m="3383620">complicated,</span>
  <span m="3384400">so</span> <span m="3384520">I</span> <span m="3384610">will</span>
  <span m="3384790">say</span> <span m="3385030">this</span> <span m="3385240">is</span>
  <span m="3385800">a</span> <span m="3385990">little</span> <span m="3386170">bit</span>
  <span m="3386290">tricky.</span> <span m="3386840">There</span> <span m="3387010">is</span>
  <span m="3388360">a</span> <span m="3388420">tendency</span> <span m="3389290">for</span>
  <span m="3390310">these</span> <span m="3390640">airplanes</span> <span m="3391510">to</span>
  <span m="3391720">turn</span> <span m="3392530">left.</span> <span m="3393770">And</span>
  <span m="3393940">there</span> <span m="3394020">are</span> <span m="3394090">actually</span>
  <span m="3394660">multiple</span> <span m="3395260">things</span> <span m="3395620">that</span>
  <span m="3395740">contribute</span> <span m="3396370">to</span> <span m="3396520">this</span>
  <span m="3397090">left-turning</span> <span m="3398170">tendency.</span> <span m="3399460">And</span>
  <span m="3399610">when</span> <span m="3399790">you're</span> <span m="3399940">in</span>
  <span m="3400120">an</span> <span m="3400210">airplane</span> <span m="3401110">flying,</span>
  <span m="3401620">you</span> <span m="3401740">might</span> <span m="3401950">hear</span>
  <span m="3402580">your</span> <span m="3402730">instructor</span> <span m="3403270">say</span>
  <span m="3403930">right</span> <span m="3404200">rudder.</span> <span m="3405350">And</span>
  <span m="3405490">it</span> <span m="3405790">is</span> <span m="3405970">really</span>
  <span m="3406210">to</span> <span m="3406300">counteract</span> <span m="3407170">some</span>
  <span m="3407410">of</span> <span m="3407470">these</span> <span m="3407710">left-turning</span>
  <span m="3408550">tendencies.</span></p><p><span m="3409510">So</span> <span m="3409660">we're</span>
  <span m="3409810">going</span> <span m="3409930">to</span> <span m="3409990">break</span>
  <span m="3410740">them</span> <span m="3410890">down</span> <span m="3411380">and</span>
  <span m="3411480">talk</span> <span m="3411670">about</span> <span m="3411940">them.</span>
  <span m="3413110">But</span> <span m="3413290">this</span> <span m="3413500">can</span>
  <span m="3413650">be</span> <span m="3413770">a</span> <span m="3413800">very</span>
  <span m="3414070">in-depth</span> <span m="3414580">subject,</span> <span m="3415180">so</span>
  <span m="3415330">I</span> <span m="3415450">will</span> <span m="3415600">definitely</span>
  <span m="3416110">refer</span> <span m="3416590">to</span> <span m="3416890">the</span>
  <span m="3417190">PHAK,</span> <span m="3418120">which</span> <span m="3418360">is</span>
  <span m="3418480">the</span> <span m="3418600"><i>Pilot</i></span> <span m="3419020"><i>Handbook</i></span>
  <span m="3419470"><i>of</i></span> <span m="3419590"><i>Aeronautical</i></span>
  <span m="3420520"><i>Knowledge.</i></span> <span m="3421240">Chapter</span> <span

  <span m="3422890">all</span> <span m="3423550">of</span> <span m="3423640">these.</span></p><p><span
  m="3424640">So</span> <span m="3424690">the</span> <span m="3424810">first</span>
  <span m="3425170">one</span> <span m="3425350">is</span> <span m="3425590">torque.</span>
  <span m="3427070">So</span> <span m="3427250">basically,</span> <span m="3428120">the</span>
  <span m="3428180">thing</span> <span m="3428450">is</span> <span m="3428630">when</span>
  <span m="3428810">you're--</span> <span m="3429230">if</span> <span m="3429650">you're</span>
  <span m="3429770">sitting</span> <span m="3430160">in</span> <span m="3430850">the</span>
  <span m="3430940">airplane,</span> <span m="3431360">and</span> <span m="3431510">you're</span>
  <span m="3431630">looking</span> <span m="3431990">forward</span> <span m="3432470">at</span>
  <span m="3432590">your</span> <span m="3432860">propeller,</span> <span m="3434000">most</span>
  <span m="3434930">US</span> <span m="3436280">engines</span> <span m="3436730">actually</span>
  <span m="3437030">have</span> <span m="3437180">the</span> <span m="3437270">propeller</span>
  <span m="3438110">rotating</span> <span m="3438860">clockwise.</span> <span m="3439910">So</span>
  <span m="3440130">and</span> <span m="3440600">you</span> <span m="3440690">can</span>
  <span m="3440840">see</span> <span m="3440960">that</span> <span m="3441170">arrow</span>
  <span m="3441500">that</span> <span m="3441650">says</span> <span m="3441950">action.</span>
  <span m="3442910">That's</span> <span m="3443120">the</span> <span m="3443210">propeller</span>
  <span m="3443720">rotating</span> <span m="3444260">clockwise.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="3448670">know</span> <span m="3449060">for</span> <span m="3449240">every</span>
  <span m="3449480">action,</span> <span m="3450060">there's</span> <span m="3450170">an</span>

  <span m="3453650">right,</span> <span m="3454190">the</span> <span m="3454280">whole</span>

  <span m="3456440">the</span> <span m="3456560">left.</span> <span m="3457070">So</span>

  <span m="3557520">the</span> <span m="3557670">airplane.</span> <span m="3559740">Does</span>
  <span m="3559830">that</span> <span m="3559980">make</span> <span m="3560160">sense?</span>
  <span m="3564370">Great.</span> <span m="3564740">Lot</span> <span m="3564970">of</span>

  <span m="3569110">time</span> <span m="3569350">getting</span> <span m="3569590">our</span>
  <span m="3569680">heads</span> <span m="3569920">around.</span> <span m="3570760">And</span>

  <span m="3586230">that</span> <span m="3586500">propeller</span> <span m="3587440">remember</span>
